### **3\. E-E-A-T Validator Module**

Copy  
/\*\*  
 \* DoorillioEEATValidator.js  
 \* E-E-A-T (Experience, Expertise, Authoritativeness, Trustworthiness) validator for Doorillio CMS  
 \*/

class DoorillioEEATValidator {  
    constructor() {  
        this.content \= '';  
        this.title \= '';  
        this.analysisResults \= {};  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Set the content to analyze  
     \*/  
    setContent(content, title) {  
        this.content \= content;  
        this.title \= title;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Run comprehensive E-E-A-T analysis  
     \*/  
    runAnalysis() {  
        if (\!this.content || \!this.title) {  
            return {  
                success: false,  
                message: 'Missing required information for analysis'  
            };  
        }  
          
        // Initialize analysis results  
        this.analysisResults \= {  
            overallScore: 0,  
            expertise: {  
                score: 0,  
                strengths: \[\],  
                weaknesses: \[\],  
                suggestions: \[\]  
            },  
            experience: {  
                score: 0,  
                strengths: \[\],  
                weaknesses: \[\],  
                suggestions: \[\]  
            },  
            authoritativeness: {  
                score: 0,  
                strengths: \[\],  
                weaknesses: \[\],  
                suggestions: \[\]  
            },  
            trustworthiness: {  
                score: 0,  
                strengths: \[\],  
                weaknesses: \[\],  
                suggestions: \[\]  
            }  
        };  
          
        // Run individual analysis checks  
        this.analyzeExpertise();  
        this.analyzeExperience();  
        this.analyzeAuthoritativeness();  
        this.analyzeTrustworthiness();  
          
        // Calculate overall score  
        this.analysisResults.overallScore \= Math.round(  
            (this.analysisResults.expertise.score \+  
            this.analysisResults.experience.score \+  
            this.analysisResults.authoritativeness.score \+  
            this.analysisResults.trustworthiness.score) / 4  
        );  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'E-E-A-T analysis completed',  
            data: this.analysisResults  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Analyze Expertise component of E-E-A-T  
     \*/  
    analyzeExpertise() {  
        let score \= 0;  
        const strengths \= \[\];  
        const weaknesses \= \[\];  
        const suggestions \= \[\];  
          
        // Check for expert quotes  
        const expertQuotes \= (this.content.match(/\<blockquote class="expert-quote"\>/g) || \[\]).length;  
          
        if (expertQuotes \>= 3) {  
            score \+= 30;  
            strengths.push('Multiple expert quotes enhance credibility');  
        } else if (expertQuotes \>= 1) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Expert quote(s) add credibility');  
            suggestions.push('Include additional expert quotes to further enhance expertise signals');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No expert quotes found');  
            suggestions.push('Include quotes from subject matter experts to enhance expertise signals');  
        }  
          
        // Check for research citations  
        const researchCitations \= (this.content.match(/\<p class="research-citation"\>/g) || \[\]).length;  
          
        if (researchCitations \>= 3) {  
            score \+= 30;  
            strengths.push('Multiple research citations demonstrate scientific backing');  
        } else if (researchCitations \>= 1) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Research citation(s) provide scientific backing');  
            suggestions.push('Include additional research citations to further enhance expertise signals');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No research citations found');  
            suggestions.push('Include citations from peer-reviewed studies or authoritative sources');  
        }  
          
        // Check for technical language and terminology  
        const termCount \= this.countTechnicalTerms();  
          
        if (termCount \>= 5) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Appropriate use of domain-specific terminology');  
        } else if (termCount \>= 2) {  
            score \+= 10;  
            strengths.push('Some domain-specific terminology present');  
            suggestions.push('Incorporate more technical terms relevant to the topic');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Limited use of domain-specific terminology');  
            suggestions.push('Include relevant technical terms to demonstrate subject expertise');  
        }  
          
        // Check for credentials or author expertise mentions  
        const hasAuthorCredentials \= this.content.includes('certified') ||   
                                     this.content.includes('licensed') ||   
                                     this.content.includes('degree') ||  
                                     this.content.includes('PhD') ||  
                                     this.content.includes('expert in');  
          
        if (hasAuthorCredentials) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Author credentials or expertise mentioned');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No author credentials mentioned');  
            suggestions.push('Include author credentials or qualifications related to the topic');  
        }  
          
        // Store the results  
        this.analysisResults.expertise.score \= Math.min(100, score);  
        this.analysisResults.expertise.strengths \= strengths;  
        this.analysisResults.expertise.weaknesses \= weaknesses;  
        this.analysisResults.expertise.suggestions \= suggestions;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Analyze Experience component of E-E-A-T  
     \*/  
    analyzeExperience() {  
        let score \= 0;  
        const strengths \= \[\];  
        const weaknesses \= \[\];  
        const suggestions \= \[\];  
          
        // Check for first-person accounts or personal experiences  
        const hasFirstPersonExperience \= this.content.includes('I have') ||   
                                         this.content.includes('my experience') ||   
                                         this.content.includes('in my practice') ||  
                                         this.content.includes('I found') ||  
                                         this.content.includes('I recommend');  
          
        if (hasFirstPersonExperience) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Personal experience or first-hand knowledge demonstrated');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No personal experience or first-hand knowledge demonstrated');  
            suggestions.push('Include personal experiences or first-hand observations related to the topic');  
        }  
          
        // Check for practical examples or case studies  
        const hasPracticalExamples \= this.content.includes('for example') ||   
                                     this.content.includes('case study') ||   
                                     this.content.includes('in practice') ||  
                                     this.content.includes('real-world example');  
          
        if (hasPracticalExamples) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Practical examples or case studies included');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No practical examples or case studies');  
            suggestions.push('Include real-world examples or case studies to demonstrate applied knowledge');  
        }  
          
        // Check for addressing common questions or pain points  
        const addressesQuestions \= this.content.includes('common question') ||   
                                   this.content.includes('frequently asked') ||   
                                   this.content.includes('many people wonder') ||  
                                   this.content.includes('common concern');  
          
        if (addressesQuestions) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Addresses common questions or concerns from experience');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Does not address common questions or concerns');  
            suggestions.push('Include sections that address common questions or concerns based on experience');  
        }  
          
        // Check for practical tips or actionable advice  
        const hasPracticalTips \= this.content.includes('tip:') ||   
                                 this.content.includes('recommendation:') ||   
                                 this.content.includes('best practice:') ||  
                                 this.content.includes('here\\'s how');  
          
        if (hasPracticalTips) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Practical tips or actionable advice from experience included');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Limited practical tips or actionable advice');  
            suggestions.push('Provide specific, actionable tips based on experience with the topic');  
        }  
          
        // Store the results  
        this.analysisResults.experience.score \= Math.min(100, score);  
        this.analysisResults.experience.strengths \= strengths;  
        this.analysisResults.experience.weaknesses \= weaknesses;  
        this.analysisResults.experience.suggestions \= suggestions;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Analyze Authoritativeness component of E-E-A-T  
     \*/  
    analyzeAuthoritativeness() {  
        let score \= 0;  
        const strengths \= \[\];  
        const weaknesses \= \[\];  
        const suggestions \= \[\];  
          
        // Check for citations from authoritative sources  
        const hasAuthoritativeCitations \= this.content.includes('according to') ||   
                                         this.content.includes('study published in') ||   
                                         this.content.includes('research from');  
          
        if (hasAuthoritativeCitations) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Citations from authoritative sources included');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No citations from authoritative sources');  
            suggestions.push('Include citations from recognized authorities or institutions in the field');  
        }  
          
        // Check for links to authoritative sites  
        const externalLinkCount \= (this.content.match(/href="http/g) || \[\]).length;  
          
        if (externalLinkCount \>= 3) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Multiple links to authoritative external sources');  
        } else if (externalLinkCount \>= 1) {  
            score \+= 15;  
            strengths.push('Links to external sources present');  
            suggestions.push('Include more links to authoritative sources to enhance authoritativeness');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('No links to authoritative external sources');  
            suggestions.push('Add links to respected organizations, studies, or resources');  
        }  
          
        // Check for comprehensive coverage of the topic  
        const wordCount \= this.countWords(this.content);  
        const headingCount \= (this.content.match(/\<h2\>/g) || \[\]).length \+ (this.content.match(/\<h3\>/g) || \[\]).length;  
          
        if (wordCount \>= 1500 && headingCount \>= 5) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Comprehensive coverage of the topic with logical structure');  
        } else if (wordCount \>= 1000) {  
            score \+= 15;  
            strengths.push('Substantial content provided on the topic');  
            suggestions.push('Expand coverage with additional subtopics or aspects of the main topic');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Coverage of the topic is not comprehensive');  
            suggestions.push('Provide more comprehensive coverage of all aspects of the topic');  
        }  
          
        // Check for mentioning different perspectives or approaches  
        const hasDifferentPerspectives \= this.content.includes('however') ||   
                                        this.content.includes('on the other hand') ||   
                                        this.content.includes('alternatively') ||  
                                        this.content.includes('different approach');  
          
        if (hasDifferentPerspectives) {  
            score \+= 25;  
            strengths.push('Different perspectives or approaches are presented');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Limited presentation of different perspectives');  
            suggestions.push('Include different viewpoints or approaches to demonstrate comprehensive understanding');  
        }  
          
        // Store the results  
        this.analysisResults.authoritativeness.score \= Math.min(100, score);  
        this.analysisResults.authoritativeness.strengths \= strengths;  
        this.analysisResults.authoritativeness.weaknesses \= weaknesses;  
        this.analysisResults.authoritativeness.suggestions \= suggestions;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Analyze Trustworthiness component of E-E-A-T  
     \*/  
    analyzeTrustworthiness() {  
        let score \= 0;  
        const strengths \= \[\];  
        const weaknesses \= \[\];  
        const suggestions \= \[\];  
          
        // Check for transparency in claims and sources  
        const hasClearSources \= this.content.includes('according to') ||   
                               this.content.includes('cited in') ||   
                               this.content.includes('published in') ||  
                               this.content.includes('researchers found');  
          
        if (hasClearSources) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Clear attribution of information to sources');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Limited attribution of information to sources');  
            suggestions.push('Clearly attribute claims and statistics to their original sources');  
        }  
          
        // Check for balanced presentation of information  
        const hasBalancedPresentation \= this.content.includes('benefits and drawbacks') ||   
                                      this.content.includes('pros and cons') ||   
                                      this.content.includes('advantages and limitations');  
          
        if (hasBalancedPresentation) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Balanced presentation of information');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Could improve balance in presentation of information');  
            suggestions.push('Include both benefits and limitations to present a balanced view');  
        }  
          
        // Check for addressing potential concerns or limitations  
        const addressesConcerns \= this.content.includes('limitation') ||   
                                this.content.includes('caution') ||   
                                this.content.includes('important to note') ||  
                                this.content.includes('consider');  
          
        if (addressesConcerns) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Addresses potential concerns or limitations');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Does not address potential concerns or limitations');  
            suggestions.push('Include sections addressing potential concerns, risks, or limitations');  
        }  
          
        // Check for clarity in distinguishing facts from opinions  
        const distinguishesFacts \= this.content.includes('research shows') ||   
                                  this.content.includes('studies indicate') ||   
                                  this.content.includes('according to data') ||  
                                  this.content.includes('evidence suggests');  
          
        const indicatesOpinions \= this.content.includes('in my opinion') ||   
                                this.content.includes('I believe') ||   
                                this.content.includes('many experts think');  
          
        if (distinguishesFacts && indicatesOpinions) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Clear distinction between facts and opinions');  
        } else if (distinguishesFacts) {  
            score \+= 15;  
            strengths.push('Clearly presents factual information');  
            suggestions.push('Ensure opinions are clearly labeled as such');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Could improve clarity in distinguishing facts from opinions');  
            suggestions.push('Clearly indicate when presenting facts versus opinions or recommendations');  
        }  
          
        // Check for recency and currency of information  
        const indicatesRecency \= this.content.includes('recent study') ||   
                               this.content.includes('latest research') ||   
                               this.content.includes('current guidelines') ||  
                               this.content.includes('2024') ||  
                               this.content.includes('2023');  
          
        if (indicatesRecency) {  
            score \+= 20;  
            strengths.push('Includes recent and current information');  
        } else {  
            weaknesses.push('Limited indication of information recency');  
            suggestions.push('Include recent studies and current information with dates');  
        }  
          
        // Store the results  
        this.analysisResults.trustworthiness.score \= Math.min(100, score);  
        this.analysisResults.trustworthiness.strengths \= strengths;  
        this.analysisResults.trustworthiness.weaknesses \= weaknesses;  
        this.analysisResults.trustworthiness.suggestions \= suggestions;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Count technical terms in the content  
     \*/  
    countTechnicalTerms() {  
        // This is a simplified approach. In a real implementation,  
        // you would have a more comprehensive list of domain-specific terms.  
        const technicalTerms \= \[  
            'metabolism', 'nutrient', 'antioxidant', 'inflammation', 'cardiovascular',  
            'protein synthesis', 'microbiome', 'flavonoid', 'polyphenol', 'bioavailability',  
            'neurotransmitter', 'glucoregulation', 'omega-3 fatty acid', 'chromium',  
            'folate', 'phytonutrient', 'catechin', 'anthocyanin', 'lycopene', 'lutein'  
        \];  
          
        let count \= 0;  
        const lowerContent \= this.content.toLowerCase();  
          
        technicalTerms.forEach(term \=\> {  
            if (lowerContent.includes(term.toLowerCase())) {  
                count++;  
            }  
        });  
          
        return count;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to count words in text  
     \*/  
    countWords(text) {  
        // Remove HTML tags  
        const strippedText \= text.replace(/\<\[^\>\]\*\>/g, ' ');  
        // Remove extra spaces and split by spaces  
        const words \= strippedText.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ').trim().split(' ');  
        return words.length;  
    }  
}

class DoorillioContentScraper {

    /\*\*

        // In a real implementation, this would use actual web scraping  
        // through libraries like Cheerio, Puppeteer, or via an API service  
          
        // Simulate API processing time  
        await this.simulateProcessing(2000);  
          
        // Generate mock scraped content based on the URL  
        const content \= this.generateMockScrapedContent(url);  
          
        // Store the scraped content  
        this.scrapedContent\[url\] \= content;  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content scraped successfully',  
            data: {  
                url: url,  
                title: content.title,  
                content: content.content,  
                publishDate: content.publishDate,  
                author: content.author  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Analyze competitors' content on a specific topic  
     \*/  
    async analyzeCompetitors(topic, maxCompetitors \= 3) {  
        console.log("Analyzing competitors for: " \+ topic);  
          
        // In a real implementation, this would first search for top content  
        // then scrape and analyze each competitor's content  
          
        // Simulate API processing time  
        await this.simulateProcessing(3000);  
          
        // Generate mock competitor analysis  
        const competitors \= this.generateMockCompetitorAnalysis(topic, maxCompetitors);  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Competitor analysis completed',  
            data: {  
                topic: topic,  
                competitors: competitors  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate mock search results  
     \*/  
    generateMockSearchResults(query, maxResults) {  
        const domains \= \[  
            'healthline.com',  
            'medicalnewstoday.com',  
            'webmd.com',  
            'mayoclinic.org',  
            'nih.gov',  
            'verywellhealth.com',  
            'health.harvard.edu',  
            'medlineplus.gov',  
            'clevelandclinic.org',  
            'hopkinsmedicine.org'  
        \];  
          
        const results \= \[\];  
          
        for (let i \= 0; i \< maxResults; i++) {  
            const domain \= domains\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* domains.length)\];  
            const title \= this.generateTitleFromQuery(query);  
            const url \= \`https://www.${domain}/${query.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, '-')}\`;  
              
            results.push({  
                title: title,  
                url: url,  
                snippet: \`Learn about ${query} and discover the latest research on this important health topic. Our comprehensive guide covers everything you need to know about ${query.toLowerCase()}.\`,  
                domain: domain,  
                publishDate: this.generateRandomDate(new Date(2023, 0, 1), new Date())  
            });  
        }  
          
        return results;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a title from a query  
     \*/  
    generateTitleFromQuery(query) {  
        const prefixes \= \[  
            'The Complete Guide to',  
            'Everything You Need to Know About',  
            'Understanding',  
            'A Comprehensive Overview of',  
            'The Health Benefits of',  
            'The Ultimate Guide to',  
            'The Science Behind',  
            'How to Improve Your Health with',  
            'Top 10 Benefits of',  
            'The Medical Perspective on'  
        \];  
          
        const prefix \= prefixes\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* prefixes.length)\];  
        return \`${prefix} ${query}\`;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate mock scraped content  
     \*/  
    generateMockScrapedContent(url) {  
        const domain \= new URL(url).hostname.replace('www.', '');  
        const path \= new URL(url).pathname;  
        const topic \= path.split('/').pop().replace(/-/g, ' ');  
          
        return {  
            title: this.generateTitleFromQuery(topic),  
            content: \`\<article\>  
                \<p\>This would be the full content scraped from ${domain} about ${topic}. In a real implementation, this would contain the actual content from the page, properly parsed and cleaned.\</p\>  
                \<p\>The content would include multiple paragraphs, headings, lists, and possibly images, all structured according to the original article's layout.\</p\>  
                \<h2\>Key Points About ${topic}\</h2\>  
                \<ul\>  
                    \<li\>Important fact \#1 about ${topic}\</li\>  
                    \<li\>Important fact \#2 about ${topic}\</li\>  
                    \<li\>Important fact \#3 about ${topic}\</li\>  
                \</ul\>  
                \<p\>Additional details would be included here, with information relevant to the query.\</p\>  
                \<h2\>Expert Opinions\</h2\>  
                \<p\>Quotes from experts would be extracted here if present in the original article.\</p\>  
                \<h2\>Scientific Research\</h2\>  
                \<p\>Citations and references to scientific studies would be included here.\</p\>  
            \</article\>\`,  
            publishDate: this.generateRandomDate(new Date(2023, 0, 1), new Date()),  
            author: this.generateRandomAuthor()  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate mock competitor analysis  
     \*/  
    generateMockCompetitorAnalysis(topic, maxCompetitors) {  
        const domains \= \[  
            'healthline.com',  
            'medicalnewstoday.com',  
            'webmd.com',  
            'mayoclinic.org',  
            'verywellhealth.com'  
        \];  
          
        const competitors \= \[\];  
          
        for (let i \= 0; i \< maxCompetitors; i++) {  
            const domain \= domains\[i\];  
            const title \= this.generateTitleFromQuery(topic);  
            const url \= \`https://www.${domain}/${topic.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, '-')}\`;  
              
            competitors.push({  
                competitor: domain,  
                url: url,  
                title: title,  
                wordCount: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 1500) \+ 1000,  
                keywordDensity: (Math.random() \* 2 \+ 1).toFixed(2) \+ '%',  
                publishDate: this.generateRandomDate(new Date(2023, 0, 1), new Date()),  
                contentStructure: this.generateMockContentStructure(),  
                keypoints: \[  
                    \`Key point \#1 about ${topic}\`,  
                    \`Key point \#2 about ${topic}\`,  
                    \`Key point \#3 about ${topic}\`  
                \],  
                estimatedTraffic: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 100000) \+ 50000  
            });  
        }  
          
        return competitors;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a random date between two dates  
     \*/  
    generateRandomDate(start, end) {  
        return new Date(start.getTime() \+ Math.random() \* (end.getTime() \- start.getTime())).toISOString().split('T')\[0\];  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a random author name  
     \*/  
    generateRandomAuthor() {  
        const firstNames \= \['John', 'Sarah', 'Michael', 'Jessica', 'David', 'Emily', 'Robert', 'Jennifer', 'William', 'Lisa'\];  
        const lastNames \= \['Smith', 'Johnson', 'Williams', 'Brown', 'Jones', 'Miller', 'Davis', 'Garcia', 'Rodriguez', 'Wilson'\];  
        const credentials \= \['MD', 'PhD', 'RD', 'MPH', 'MS', 'RN', 'LCSW', 'PT', 'OT', 'PharmD'\];  
          
        const firstName \= firstNames\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* firstNames.length)\];  
        const lastName \= lastNames\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* lastNames.length)\];  
        const credential \= credentials\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* credentials.length)\];  
          
        return \`${firstName} ${lastName}, ${credential}\`;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a mock content structure  
     \*/  
    generateMockContentStructure() {  
        return {  
            headings: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 5) \+ 3,  
            paragraphs: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 10) \+ 10,  
            images: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 5) \+ 1,  
            lists: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 3) \+ 1,  
            tables: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 2),  
            expertQuotes: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 3)  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to simulate API processing time  
     \*/  
    simulateProcessing(ms) {  
        return new Promise(resolve \=\> setTimeout(resolve, ms));  
    }  
}

// Export for use in other modules  
if (typeof module \!== 'undefined') {  
    module.exports \= DoorillioContentScraper;  
}

            \],

                'Incorporating Mindfulness in',  
                'The Art of Living with',  
                'Transforming Your Life Through',  
                'Simple Ways to Embrace'  
            \]  
        };  
          
        const suffixes \= {  
            'Nutrition': \[  
                'a Balanced Diet',  
                'Healthy Eating',  
                'Meal Planning',  
                'Nutritional Supplements',  
                'Plant-Based Proteins',  
                'Anti-Inflammatory Foods',

                'Strength Training',  
                'Cardiovascular Health',

                'Recovery Techniques',  
                'Home Workouts',  
                'Weight Management',  
                'Sports Performance',  
                'Functional Training'  
            \],  
            'Mental Health': \[  
                'Mindfulness Meditation',  
                'Stress Reduction',  
                'Sleep Quality',  
                'Work-Life Balance',  
                'Emotional Intelligence',  
                'Cognitive Behavioral Techniques',  
                'Digital Detox',  
                'Relationship Building'  
            \],  
            'Health & Wellness': \[  
                'Preventive Healthcare',  
                'Immune System Support',  
                'Natural Healing',  
                'Energy Enhancement',  
                'Chronic Pain Management',  
                'Detoxification',  
                'Seasonal Health',  
                'Aging Gracefully'  
            \],  
            'Lifestyle': \[  
                'Sustainable Living',  
                'Personal Development',  
                'Time Management',  
                'Creative Expression',  
                'Social Connections',  
                'Environmental Wellness',  
                'Financial Wellbeing',  
                'Minimalist Practices'  
            \]  
        };  
          
        // If category is provided, use its specific prefixes and suffixes  
        if (category && prefixes\[category\] && suffixes\[category\]) {  
            const prefix \= prefixes\[category\]\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* prefixes\[category\].length)\];  
            const suffix \= suffixes\[category\]\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* suffixes\[category\].length)\];  
            return \`${prefix} ${suffix}\`;  
        }   
        // Otherwise, pick a random category  
        else {  
            const allCategories \= Object.keys(prefixes);  
            const randomCategory \= allCategories\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* allCategories.length)\];  
            const prefix \= prefixes\[randomCategory\]\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* prefixes\[randomCategory\].length)\];  
            const suffix \= suffixes\[randomCategory\]\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* suffixes\[randomCategory\].length)\];  
            return \`${prefix} ${suffix}\`;

    }

        const lastNames \= \['Smith', 'Johnson', 'Williams', 'Brown', 'Jones', 'Miller', 'Davis', 'Garcia', 'Rodriguez', 'Wilson'\];  
        const credentials \= \['MD', 'PhD', 'RD', 'MPH', 'MS', 'RN', 'LCSW', 'PT', 'OT', 'PharmD'\];  
          
        const firstName \= firstNames\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* firstNames.length)\];  
        const lastName \= lastNames\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* lastNames.length)\];  
        const credential \= Math.random() \> 0.5 ? credentials\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* credentials.length)\] : '';  
          
        return credential ? \`${firstName} ${lastName}, ${credential}\` : \`${firstName} ${lastName}\`;  
    }

### **6\. Content Planner Module**

Copy  
/\*\*  
 \* DoorillioContentPlanner.js  
 \* Module for planning and scheduling content  
 \*/

class DoorillioContentPlanner {  
    constructor() {  
        this.contentCalendar \= \[\];  
        this.contentStrategy \= {};  
        this.contentPillars \= \[\];  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Initialize content strategy  
     \*/  
    initializeStrategy(strategy) {  
        console.log("Initializing content strategy: " \+ strategy.name);  
          
        this.contentStrategy \= {  
            name: strategy.name,  
            description: strategy.description,  
            startDate: strategy.startDate,  
            endDate: strategy.endDate,  
            goals: strategy.goals || \[\],  
            targetAudience: strategy.targetAudience || \[\],  
            focusKeywords: strategy.focusKeywords || \[\],  
            contentTypes: strategy.contentTypes || \[\],  
            status: strategy.status || 'Active'  
        };  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content strategy initialized successfully',  
            data: this.contentStrategy  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Set up content pillars  
     \*/  
    setupContentPillars(pillars) {  
        console.log("Setting up content pillars");  
          
        this.contentPillars \= pillars.map(pillar \=\> ({  
            id: pillar.id || this.generateId('pillar'),  
            name: pillar.name,  
            description: pillar.description || '',  
            category: pillar.category || '',  
            focusKeywords: pillar.focusKeywords || \[\],  
            status: pillar.status || 'Active',  
            subpillars: pillar.subpillars || \[\]  
        }));  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content pillars set up successfully',  
            data: {  
                pillars: this.contentPillars  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Add subpillar to existing pillar  
     \*/  
    addSubpillar(pillarId, subpillar) {  
        console.log(\`Adding subpillar "${subpillar.name}" to pillar ${pillarId}\`);  
          
        const pillarIndex \= this.contentPillars.findIndex(p \=\> p.id \=== pillarId);  
          
        if (pillarIndex \=== \-1) {  
            return {  
                success: false,  
                message: 'Pillar not found'  
            };  
        }  
          
        const newSubpillar \= {  
            id: subpillar.id || this.generateId('subpillar'),  
            name: subpillar.name,  
            description: subpillar.description || '',  
            focusKeyword: subpillar.focusKeyword || '',  
            secondaryKeywords: subpillar.secondaryKeywords || \[\],  
            status: subpillar.status || 'Not Started'  
        };  
          
        this.contentPillars\[pillarIndex\].subpillars.push(newSubpillar);  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Subpillar added successfully',  
            data: {  
                pillar: this.contentPillars\[pillarIndex\],  
                subpillar: newSubpillar  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Plan content calendar  
     \*/  
    planContentCalendar(startDate, endDate, frequency \= 'weekly') {  
        console.log(\`Planning content calendar from ${startDate} to ${endDate}\`);  
          
        // Clear existing calendar  
        this.contentCalendar \= \[\];  
          
        // Parse dates  
        const start \= new Date(startDate);  
        const end \= new Date(endDate);  
          
        // Calculate publishing dates based on frequency  
        const dates \= \[\];  
        let currentDate \= new Date(start);  
          
        while (currentDate \<= end) {  
            dates.push(new Date(currentDate));  
              
            // Increment based on frequency  
            if (frequency \=== 'daily') {  
                currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() \+ 1);  
            } else if (frequency \=== 'weekly') {  
                currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() \+ 7);  
            } else if (frequency \=== 'biweekly') {  
                currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() \+ 14);  
            } else if (frequency \=== 'monthly') {  
                currentDate.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() \+ 1);  
            }  
        }  
          
        // Assign content to dates  
        // Prioritize subpillars that haven't been started  
        let pendingSubpillars \= \[\];  
          
        this.contentPillars.forEach(pillar \=\> {  
            pillar.subpillars.forEach(subpillar \=\> {  
                if (subpillar.status \=== 'Not Started') {  
                    pendingSubpillars.push({  
                        pillarId: pillar.id,  
                        pillarName: pillar.name,  
                        subpillarId: subpillar.id,  
                        subpillarName: subpillar.name,  
                        focusKeyword: subpillar.focusKeyword  
                    });  
                }  
            });  
        });  
          
        // Shuffle pending subpillars to distribute content evenly  
        pendingSubpillars \= this.shuffleArray(pendingSubpillars);  
          
        // Create calendar entries  
        dates.forEach((date, index) \=\> {  
            const subpillar \= pendingSubpillars\[index % pendingSubpillars.length\];  
              
            this.contentCalendar.push({  
                id: this.generateId('calendar'),  
                date: date.toISOString().split('T')\[0\],  
                pillarId: subpillar.pillarId,  
                pillarName: subpillar.pillarName,  
                subpillarId: subpillar.subpillarId,  
                subpillarName: subpillar.subpillarName,  
                contentTitle: this.generateContentTitle(subpillar.subpillarName, subpillar.focusKeyword),  
                focusKeyword: subpillar.focusKeyword,  
                contentType: this.getRandomContentType(),  
                status: 'Planned',  
                assignedTo: ''  
            });  
        });  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content calendar planned successfully',  
            data: {  
                calendar: this.contentCalendar,  
                startDate: startDate,  
                endDate: endDate,  
                frequency: frequency,  
                totalEntries: this.contentCalendar.length  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Get content calendar  
     \*/  
    getContentCalendar(month \= null, year \= null) {  
        console.log("Getting content calendar");  
          
        let filteredCalendar \= \[...this.contentCalendar\];  
          
        // Filter by month and year if provided  
        if (month \!== null && year \!== null) {  
            const monthStr \= month.toString().padStart(2, '0');  
            const yearStr \= year.toString();  
            const datePrefix \= \`${yearStr}\-${monthStr}\`;  
              
            filteredCalendar \= filteredCalendar.filter(entry \=\>   
                entry.date.startsWith(datePrefix)  
            );  
        }  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content calendar retrieved successfully',  
            data: {  
                calendar: filteredCalendar  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Update calendar entry  
     \*/  
    updateCalendarEntry(entryId, updatedData) {  
        console.log(\`Updating calendar entry ${entryId}\`);  
          
        const entryIndex \= this.contentCalendar.findIndex(entry \=\> entry.id \=== entryId);  
          
        if (entryIndex \=== \-1) {  
            return {  
                success: false,  
                message: 'Calendar entry not found'  
            };  
        }  
          
        // Update the entry with new data  
        this.contentCalendar\[entryIndex\] \= {  
            ...this.contentCalendar\[entryIndex\],  
            ...updatedData,  
            id: entryId // Ensure ID remains the same  
        };  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Calendar entry updated successfully',  
            data: {  
                entry: this.contentCalendar\[entryIndex\]  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Find content gaps  
     \*/  
    findContentGaps() {  
        console.log("Finding content gaps");  
          
        const gaps \= \[\];  
          
        // Check each pillar for incomplete subpillars  
        this.contentPillars.forEach(pillar \=\> {  
            const notStartedSubpillars \= pillar.subpillars.filter(sp \=\> sp.status \=== 'Not Started');  
              
            if (notStartedSubpillars.length \> 0) {  
                gaps.push({  
                    pillar: pillar.name,  
                    missingContent: notStartedSubpillars.map(sp \=\> sp.name),  
                    priority: 'High',  
                    suggestion: \`Create content for ${notStartedSubpillars.length} missing subpillars in ${pillar.name}\`  
                });  
            }  
        });  
          
        // Add additional gap types  
        gaps.push({  
            pillar: 'Mental Health',  
            missingContent: \['Anxiety Management', 'Depression Awareness'\],  
            priority: 'Medium',  
            suggestion: 'Add content addressing anxiety management and depression awareness'  
        });  
          
        gaps.push({  
            pillar: 'Nutrition',  
            missingContent: \['Plant-Based Diets', 'Food Allergies'\],  
            priority: 'High',  
            suggestion: 'Develop comprehensive guides on plant-based diets and food allergies'  
        });  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content gaps identified',  
            data: {  
                gaps: gaps,  
                totalGaps: gaps.length  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Generate a content brief  
     \*/  
    generateContentBrief(pillarId, subpillarId) {  
        console.log(\`Generating content brief for subpillar ${subpillarId}\`);  
          
        // Find the pillar and subpillar  
        const pillar \= this.contentPillars.find(p \=\> p.id \=== pillarId);  
          
        if (\!pillar) {  
            return {  
                success: false,  
                message: 'Pillar not found'  
            };  
        }  
          
        const subpillar \= pillar.subpillars.find(sp \=\> sp.id \=== subpillarId);  
          
        if (\!subpillar) {  
            return {  
                success: false,  
                message: 'Subpillar not found'  
            };  
        }  
          
        // Generate a content brief based on the pillar and subpillar  
        const brief \= {  
            title: this.generateContentTitle(subpillar.name, subpillar.focusKeyword),  
            pillar: pillar.name,  
            subpillar: subpillar.name,  
            targetKeyword: subpillar.focusKeyword,  
            secondaryKeywords: subpillar.secondaryKeywords,  
            contentType: this.getRandomContentType(),  
            wordCount: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 500) \+ 1500, // 1500-2000 words  
            targetAudience: this.contentStrategy.targetAudience || \['Health-conscious individuals', 'Fitness enthusiasts'\],  
            purpose: \`Create a comprehensive guide on ${subpillar.name} that ranks well for "${subpillar.focusKeyword}" and establishes authority in the "${pillar.name}" topic.\`,  
            outline: this.generateOutline(subpillar.name, subpillar.focusKeyword),  
            keyPoints: this.generateKeyPoints(subpillar.name),  
            references: this.generateReferences(),  
            expertQuotes: true,  
            images: Math.floor(Math.random() \* 3) \+ 3, // 3-5 images  
            internalLinkingOpportunities: this.generateInternalLinkingOpportunities(pillarId, subpillarId)  
        };  
          
        return {  
            success: true,  
            message: 'Content brief generated successfully',  
            data: {  
                brief: brief  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a unique ID  
     \*/  
    generateId(prefix \= '') {  
        return prefix \+ '\_' \+ Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a content title  
     \*/  
    generateContentTitle(subpillarName, keyword) {  
        const templates \= \[  
            \`The Complete Guide to ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`${subpillarName}: Everything You Need to Know\`,  
            \`How ${subpillarName} Can Improve Your Health\`,  
            \`${subpillarName}: Benefits, Research, and Practical Tips\`,  
            \`Why ${subpillarName} Matters for Your Wellbeing\`,  
            \`10 Ways to Incorporate ${subpillarName} Into Your Routine\`,  
            \`The Science Behind ${subpillarName} and Your Health\`,  
            \`${subpillarName}: A Comprehensive Approach\`,  
            \`Understanding ${subpillarName}: A Deep Dive\`,  
            \`${subpillarName} 101: Beginner's Guide\`  
        \];  
          
        let title \= templates\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* templates.length)\];  
          
        // Ensure the keyword is included  
        if (keyword && \!title.toLowerCase().includes(keyword.toLowerCase())) {  
            title \= title.replace(subpillarName, \`${subpillarName} for ${keyword}\`);  
        }  
          
        return title;  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to get a random content type  
     \*/  
    getRandomContentType() {  
        const contentTypes \= \[  
            'Comprehensive Guide',  
            'List Article',  
            'How-To Guide',  
            'Expert Interview',  
            'Case Study',  
            'Research Review',  
            'Comparison Article',  
            'Beginner\\'s Guide',  
            'FAQ Article',  
            'Problem-Solution Article'  
        \];  
          
        return contentTypes\[Math.floor(Math.random() \* contentTypes.length)\];  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate a basic outline  
     \*/  
    generateOutline(subpillarName, keyword) {  
        return \[  
            \`Introduction to ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`What is ${subpillarName}?\`,  
            \`The Science Behind ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Benefits of ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`How to Incorporate ${subpillarName} Into Your Routine\`,  
            \`Common Misconceptions About ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Expert Insights on ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Research and Evidence for ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Tips for Getting the Most from ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Conclusion: Next Steps with ${subpillarName}\`  
        \];  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate key points  
     \*/  
    generateKeyPoints(subpillarName) {  
        return \[  
            \`${subpillarName} has been shown to improve overall health\`,  
            \`Regular engagement with ${subpillarName} can boost well-being\`,  
            \`Many people misunderstand key aspects of ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Scientific research supports the benefits of ${subpillarName}\`,  
            \`Implementing ${subpillarName} doesn't have to be complicated\`  
        \];  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate references  
     \*/  
    generateReferences() {  
        return \[  
            { title: 'Journal of Health Studies', url: 'https://example.com/journal1' },  
            { title: 'American Health Association', url: 'https://example.com/aha' },  
            { title: 'National Institute of Health', url: 'https://example.com/nih' }  
        \];  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to generate internal linking opportunities  
     \*/  
    generateInternalLinkingOpportunities(currentPillarId, currentSubpillarId) {  
        const opportunities \= \[\];  
          
        this.contentPillars.forEach(pillar \=\> {  
            pillar.subpillars.forEach(subpillar \=\> {  
                // Don't include the current subpillar  
                if (pillar.id \=== currentPillarId && subpillar.id \=== currentSubpillarId) {  
                    return;  
                }  
                  
                // Add related subpillars as linking opportunities  
                if (subpillar.status \=== 'Complete' || subpillar.status \=== 'In Progress') {  
                    opportunities.push({  
                        pillar: pillar.name,  
                        subpillar: subpillar.name,  
                        title: this.generateContentTitle(subpillar.name, subpillar.focusKeyword),  
                        url: \`https://doorillio.com/${pillar.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, '-')}/${subpillar.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\\s+/g, '-')}\`  
                    });  
                }  
            });  
        });  
          
        // Limit to 5 opportunities  
        return this.shuffleArray(opportunities).slice(0, 5);  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Helper function to shuffle an array  
     \*/  
    shuffleArray(array) {  
        const newArray \= \[...array\];  
        for (let i \= newArray.length \- 1; i \> 0; i--) {  
            const j \= Math.floor(Math.random() \* (i \+ 1));  
            \[newArray\[i\], newArray\[j\]\] \= \[newArray\[j\], newArray\[i\]\];  
        }  
        return newArray;  
    }  
}

// Export for use in other modules  
if (typeof module \!== 'undefined') {  
    module.exports \= DoorillioContentPlanner;  
}

### **7\. Main Application Logic Module**

Copy  
/\*\*  
 \* DoorillioApp.js  
 \* Main application logic module for the Doorillio Content Generation System  
 \*/

class DoorillioApp {  
    constructor() {  
        // Initialize modules  
        this.contentGenerator \= new DoorillioContentGenerator();  
        this.seoAnalyzer \= new DoorillioSEOAnalyzer();  
        this.eeatValidator \= new DoorillioEEATValidator();  
        this.contentScraper \= new DoorillioContentScraper();  
        this.integrationManager \= new DoorillioIntegrationManager();  
        this.contentPlanner \= new DoorillioContentPlanner();  
          
        // Application state  
        this.currentProject \= null;  
        this.currentUser \= null;  
        this.appConfig \= {  
            apiKeys: {},  
            seoSettings: {  
                minWordCount: 1500,  
                optimalKeywordDensity: 0.02, // 2%  
                enableAutomaticInterlinking: true  
            },  
            contentSettings: {  
                defaultContentType: 'Comprehensive Guide',  
                includeExpertQuotes: true,  
                enableEEATOptimization: true  
            },  
            wordPressSettings: {  
                baseUrl: 'https://doorillio.com',  
                username: ''  
            }  
        };  
    }  
      
    /\*\*  
     \* Initialize the application  
     \*/  
    async initialize(config \= {}) {  
        console.log("Initializing Doorillio Content Generation System");  
          
        // Set up configuration  
        this.appConfig \= {  
            ...this.appConfig,  
            ...config  
        };  
          
        // Set API keys if provided  
        if (config.apiKeys) {  
            if (config.apiKeys.openai) {  
                this.contentGenerator.apiKey \= config.apiKeys.openai;  
            }  
              
            if (config.apiKeys.wordpress) {  
                this.integrationManager.apiKey \= config.apiKeys.wordpress;

                this.integrationManager.wpBaseUrl \= config.wordPress
